specification.\\n\\n**CSI Node Plugin Client (csi_client.go):**\\nDefines the `csiClient` interface for communicating with CSI drivers over gRPC. This interface includes methods like `NodeGetInfo()` for retrieving node capabilities and topology information, `NodePublishVolume()` for mounting volumes, and `NodeUnpublishVolume()` for unmounting. Implements the volume.Mounter interface with SetUp/TearDown operations, managing the staging and publishing of CSI volumes on nodes.\\n\\n**CSI Plugin (csi_plugin.go):**\\nThe main CSI plugin implementation that registers with Kubernetes' volume plugin system. Includes the `RegistrationHandler` for CSI driver registration and validation. Manages CSI driver discovery and initialization, storing driver endpoints in a global drivers store.\\n\\n**CSI Volume Expander (expander.go):**\\nImplements node-side volume expansion through the `NodeExpand()` method for CSI drivers. Allows volumes to be resized after provisioning.\\n\\n**CSI Node Info Manager (nodeinfomanager/nodeinfomanager.go):**\\nManages CSI node information, storing driver capabilities and node topology information in node annotations (csi.volume.kubernetes.io/nodeid). Implements CSI migration logic through `CSINameTranslator` and `CSIMigratedPluginManager` interfaces. Handles provisioning delegation to external CSI provisioners, translates in-tree plugin provisioners to CSI drivers when migration is enabled, and manages DataSource handling for clone/restore operations with CSI drivers.\\n\\n**Volume Expansion Controller Integration (expand_controller.go):**\\nIntegrates CSI migration support for volume expansion. (CSI) specification.\\n\\n**CSI Node Plugin Client (csi_client.go):**\\nDefines the `csiClient` interface for communicating with CSI drivers over gRPC. This interface includes methods like `NodeGetInfo()` for retrieving node capabilities and topology information, `NodePublishVolume()` for mounting volumes, and `NodeUnpublishVolume()` for unmounting. It serves as the primary client for all node-level CSI driver interactions.\\n\\n**CSI Volume Attach/Detach Controller (csi_attacher.go):**\\nImplements the `csiAttacher` struct that handles VolumeAttach and VolumeDetach operations. This component manages the attachment of CSI volumes to nodes and their detachment, implementing the volume.Attacher interface. It coordinates with the Kubernetes API to create/delete VolumeAttachment resources.\\n\\n**Volume Attach/Detach Controller Integration (attach_detach_controller.go):**\\nThe main attach-detach controller integrates CSI drivers through CSI node and driver listers, CSI migration managers, and the CSI plugin interface. It routes volume operations to the appropriate plugin based on the volume type and handles both in-tree and CSI driver volumes.\\n\\n**CSI Volume Mounter (csi_mounter.go):**\\nImplements the `csiMountMgr` struct that handles volume mounting operations. Implements the volume.Mounter interface with SetUp/TearDown operations, managing the staging and publishing of CSI volumes on nodes.\\n\\n**CSI Plugin (csi_plugin.go):**\\nThe main CSI plugin implementation that registers with Kubernetes' volume plugin system. Includes the `RegistrationHandler` for CSI driver registration and validation. Manages CSI driver discovery and initialization, storing driver endpoints in a global drivers store.\\n\\n**CSI Volume Expander (expander.go):**\\nImplements node-side volume expansion through the `NodeExpand()` method for CSI drivers. Allows volumes to be resized after provisioning.\\n\\n**CSI Node Info Manager (nodeinfomanager/nodeinfomanager.go):**\\nManages CSI node information, storing driver capabilities and node topology information in node annotations (csi.volume.kubernetes.io/nodeid). Updates node labels with topology information from CSI drivers.\\n\\n**CSI Storage Registry Components:**\\n- **CSIDriver Storage (csidriver/)**: Handles storage and strategy for CSIDriver API objects, managing CSI driver registration and discovery\\n- **CSINode Storage (csinode/)**: Manages CSINode objects that store node-specific CSI driver information\\n- **CSIStorageCapacity Storage (csistoragecapacity/)**: Handles storage capacity tracking for CSI drivers\\n\\n**PersistentVolume Controller Integration (pv_controller.go, pv_controller_base.go):**\\nBridges CSI driver operations to the core storage API. Implements CSI migration logic through `CSINameTranslator` and `CSIMigratedPluginManager` interfaces. Handles provisioning delegation to external CSI provisioners, translates in-tree plugin provisioners to CSI drivers when migration is enabled, and manages DataSource handling for clone/restore operations with CSI drivers.\\n\\n**Volume Expansion Controller Integration (expand_controller.go):**\\nIntegrates CSI migration support for volume expansion. Translates expansion requests for migrated in-tree plugins to CSI resizer names and coordinates with external resizers.\\n\\n**CSI Migration Plugin Manager (plugin_manager.go):**\\nManages the translation between in-tree plugin names and CSI driver names, tracks CSI migration status for plugins, and provides integration points for other controllers to determine if a plugin has been migrated to CSI.\\n\\n**Additional CSI Components:**\\n- **csi_block.go**: Implements block volume support for CSI drivers\\n- **csi_drivers_store.go**: Maintains the registry of registered CSI drivers and their endpoints\\n- **csi_metrics.go**: Provides metrics collection for CSI operations\\n- **csi_util.go**: Utility functions for CSI volume operations\\n\\nThese components work together to provide complete CSI driver integration, enabling external storage drivers to integrate with Kubernetes' storage subsystem through a standardized interface.\"\n    49→}\n    50→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware.
